so it may be that the neural mechanisms for representing the space around us are also used for generating visual imagery so that we can recreate the spatial scene , at least , of the events that have happened to us when we want to imagine them .	所以 , 也許 , 神經機制代表我們週遭的空間 , 也能用來產生視覺圖像 , 讓我們能創造出空間的場景 , 至少 , 當我們想要想像時 , 發生在我們身上的事件 。
so if this was happening , your memories could start by place cells activating each other via these dense interconnections and then reactivating boundary cells to create the spatial structure of the scene around your viewpoint .	所以如果發生了 , 你的記憶可以從位置細胞透過密集的連接開始啟動彼此 , 然後啟動邊界細胞 , 創造出你觀點周圍空間的結構 。
and grid cells could move this viewpoint through that space .	網格細胞可以透過這個空間移動這個視角 。
another kind of cell , head direction cells , which i didn't mention yet , they fire like a compass according to which way you're facing .	另外一種我還沒提到的細胞頭部方向細胞 , 它們就像指南針一樣發出信號 , 根據你面對的方向 。
they could define the viewing direction from which you want to generate an image for your visual imagery , so you can imagine what happened when you were at this wedding , for example .	他們可以定義觀看的方向 , 例如你想要為你的視覺影像產生影像 , 所以你可以想像當你在婚禮上發生什麼事 。
so this is just one example of a new era really in cognitive neuroscience where we're beginning to understand psychological processes like how you remember or imagine or even think in terms of the actions of the billions of individual neurons that make up our brains .	這只是一個新的認知神經科學領域的例子 , 我們開始了解心理學過程 , 像是你如何記得、想像 , 或甚至思考 , 根據數十億個獨立神經元所組成的大腦所採取的行動 。
thank you very much .	非常謝謝各位 。
imagine a global security driven by collaboration among agencies , government , the private sector and the public . that's not just the distant hope of opensource fans , it's the vision of james stavridis , the supreme commander of nato , who shares vivid moments from recent military history to explain why security of the future should be built with bridges rather than walls .	想像一下 , 一個全球安全的驅動力 , 是由政府部門、私營部門和大眾合作所驅動的 。 這不只是開放程式碼的希望 , 是北約大陸的詹姆士•史達維里迪斯的願景 , 北約的最高指揮官 , 他們在近期的軍事歷史上都很活躍 , 來解釋為什麼未來的安全應該要用橋樑來建造 , 而不是用牆 。
collaboration , global issues , opensource , peace , politics , social media , violence , war	合作、全球議題、開放資源、和平、政治、社交媒體、暴力、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭 。
james stavridis: how nato's supreme commander thinks about global security	詹姆斯•斯特瓦里迪斯:北約的最高指揮官如何看待全球安全的看法 。
i'm gonna talk a little bit about opensource security , because we've got to get better at security in this 21st century .	我將要談一下開放資源的安全性 , 因為在21世紀 , 我們的安全性得更好 。
let me start by saying , let's look back to the 20th century , and kind of get a sense of how that style of security worked for us .	讓我先說 , 讓我們回顧二十世紀 , 了解安全的風格對我們是如何運作的 。
this is verdun , a battlefield in france just north of the nato headquarters in belgium .	這是verdun , 法國的戰場就在北約總部的比利時 。
at verdun , in 1916 , over a 300day period , 700 , 000 people were killed , so about 2 , 000 a day .	1916年 , 在verdun , 在超過三百天的期間 , 七十萬人被殺 , 一天大約兩千人 。
if you roll it forward 20thcentury security into the second world war , you see the battle of stalingrad , 300 days , 2 million people killed .	如果你把它推向第二次世界大戰 , 你會看到史達林格的戰役 , 300天 , 兩百萬人被殺 。
we go into the cold war , and we continue to try and build walls .	我們進入冷戰 , 繼續建造牆壁 。
we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從第一次世界大戰的壕溝走到第二次世界大戰的岩石線 , 然後我們走進冷戰、鐵幕、柏林圍牆 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	我今天的論點是 , 我們不需要建造牆壁來創造安全 , 我們需要建造橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這座橋在歐洲很有名 。
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	愛佛•安德里的一座橋樑 , 談到小說的主題 , 談到歐洲和巴爾幹半島 , 長久以來一直有巨大的圍牆 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	最近 , 在過去十年 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始 , 猶豫地 , 團結起來 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我認為 , 同樣地 , 開放式安全是關於聯繫國際、跨部門、私人公共 , 和策略性溝通 , 主要是以社交網路來溝通 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	所以 , 讓我來談談為什麼我們需要這麼做 , 因為全球公有物正受到各種攻擊 , 而對全球公有物的威脅 , 都不會被建立牆壁來解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	顯然我是個水手 。
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一條線 , 橫跨整個印度洋 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	在音樂廳的一邊有電線 。
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	那是為了阻止海盜攻擊 。
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	海盜是現今全世界非常活躍的威脅 。 這是在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	海盜也在馬拉卡海峽很活躍 。
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	它在幾內亞灣很活躍 。
we see it in the caribbean .	我們在加勒比海也看到了 。
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	它是全球交通運輸系統的一百億美元損失 。
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 當時有20艘船 , 500名船員被挾持 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是對全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要考慮如何處理它 。
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉移到另一種海洋 , 網路的海洋 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這是兩個年輕人的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	此刻 , 他們被監禁 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們做了信用卡詐欺 , 騙了他們超過一百億美金 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是全球經濟損失2兆美元的網路犯罪的一部分 。
two trillion a year .	每年兩兆美元 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	這只是英國的國內生產毛額 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以 , 我們知道的網路世界是最基本的開放 , 受到很大的威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	在全球公有物中 , 我擔心的另一件事是被人口販賣所造成的威脅 , 被毒品、鴉片等毒品的運動所威脅 , 從阿富汗穿過歐洲到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心從安第斯山北邊來的古柯鹼 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器的運輸 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的成本 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	人口販賣主要在海洋上 , 但在全球公有物的其他地方 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我真希望我能告訴你們 , 這是我們用來阻止人口販賣的高科技產品 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是販毒集團的半潛水員 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	它是建在南美叢林裡的 。
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那個低科技的木筏逮捕了它它 , 它載著六噸的古柯鹼 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四個船員 。 精密的溝通會迅速掃除 。
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販運 , 在毒品、人、武器、神禁止 , 大規模毀滅的武器 , 是威脅全球公有物的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	咱們現在就一起在阿富汗 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這裡是阿富汗的一片聚集地 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	全世界百分之八十到九十的口袋裡 , 鴉片和海洛因來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	當然 , 我們也看到了恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	蓋達組織就是從這裡開始的 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到一個很強的暴動隱藏在其中 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義也是全球公有物的一部分 , 我們必須要處理的 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以現在我們來到21世紀 。
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們20世紀的工具是行不通的 。
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我認為我們不能僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不能僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們需要軍隊的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這麼做時 , 我們必須做得很好 , 且要有競爭力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放式安全是關於國際、跨部門、私人和公共的聯繫 , 透過這種在網路上的戰略溝通的概念 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子來說明這如何運作 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 , 阿富汗的士兵
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 這很奇怪 。 我想我讀到的是 , 在阿富汗的人口統計、年輕人和女性 , 大多是不識字的 。 」
you would be correct .	你是對的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗的安全部隊時 , 百分之八十五的人無法閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班在這些男人和女人學會閱讀的時期 , 保持著高等教育 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿著書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們閱讀在北約的識字課程中 , 通過與私人企業合作 , 和發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教過了超過二十萬的阿富汗安全部隊 , 要從基本的層面去閱讀和寫作 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你能讀書並在阿富汗寫字時 , 你就會把一支筆放進口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在典禮上 , 當這些年輕人畢業時 , 他們很驕傲地拿著筆 , 放進他們的口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	國際間有50個國家參與這項任務--國際間的介入--這些發展部門和私人公共部門 , 來進行這種安全 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教他們戰鬥技巧 , 但我認為 , 開放式安全意味著連結創造更持久的安全效應 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	它叫做舒適感 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘叫做慈悲的姐妹船 。
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船隻 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這個 , 舒適的是整個加勒比海以及南美洲的海岸進行病人治療
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在一般的航行中 , 他們會做四十萬個病人治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	船員不是嚴格的部隊人員 , 而是結合人道主義組織: 「 希望 」 、 「 微笑 」 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織會派出義工 。
interagency physicians come out .	跨領域的醫生出來了 。
they're all part of this .	他們都是這方面的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	給你一個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲的小男孩 , 帶著他的母親走到安慰的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被配上時 , 他突然抬起頭說: 「 媽媽 , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽媽 , 我看到世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	將這個乘以40萬的病人治療 , 這個私人和安全部門合作的力量 , 你就會開始看到創造安全的力量以非常不同的方式 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到的是棒球員 。
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能在照片中挑出兩名美國士兵嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這兩位年輕男孩一邊的年輕人 。 這是一系列棒球診所 , 我們在全美棒球聯盟、國務院、軍隊棒球隊、棒球選手之間的合作 , 他們是真正的士兵 , 參與這項任務 , 他們在拉丁美洲和加勒比海、加勒比海、加勒比海和加勒比海地區的診所 , 和加勒比海岸、加勒比海岸和加勒比海岸之間的合作 , 創造了安全感 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它向年輕人展示關於健身和女性的榜樣 , 以及關於生命的榜樣 , 我認為這能為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這種合作關係的另一面是災難救援 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是一架美國空軍直升機 , 參與了2004年的海嘯 , 殺害了25萬人 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在這些重大災難中 , 2004年的海嘯 , 25萬人死亡 , 2005年的巴基斯坦地震 , 8萬5千人死亡 , 海地地地震 , 30萬人死亡 , 最近 , 地震海嘯的組合 , 震撼了日本和它的核產業 , 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了跨國界的合作關係 , 跨國界的合作關係 , 和安全部隊合作 , 來推動這種自然災難 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	這些都是開放式安全的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們把它們綁在一起 , 透過這樣的方式增加 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在你看到的這個想法: 「 啊 , 司令 , 這些必定是通訊的航線 , 或者是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 , 這是twitter公司推出的圖表 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 , 綠色是地理位置 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	它激起了那偉大的人口調查世界第六大的國家以下順序:中國、印度、臉書、美國、推特和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們要收集這些蚊帳 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	為什麼我們想要參與其中 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們先前談過阿拉伯之春 , 以及它的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉另一個例子 , 它是如何傳遞訊息的 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦做了一個類似這樣的演講 。 我對你們說 , 我在臉書上 , 朋友 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	觀眾笑了一下 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇文章是用ap來運作的 , 用電線來播放 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	世界上有兩個地方:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北大西洋公約需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	這個故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上我有數百個臉書朋友請求 , 來自印尼和芬蘭 , 他們大多會說: 「 司令 , 我們聽說你需要一個朋友 , 喔 , 順便說一下 , 哪個是北約人 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	沒錯 , 我們會笑 , 但這就是我們如何傳遞訊息 , 轉移訊息就是我們如何連結國際、跨部門、公共和國 , 以及這些社交網路 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我說一個嚴肅的話題 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭警衛隊 。
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他現在站在helmand的手錶 , 在阿富汗南部 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我讓他來這裡提醒我們 , 我不希望任何人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要有能力、有能力的軍隊 , 來創造真正的軍事效應 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	那就是我們是誰的核心以及我們所做的事 , 我們保護自由、言論自由、以及我們在社會中珍視的一切 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道 , 人生並不是一個隨身開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有軍隊 , 要不是在戰鬥中 , 就是在倉庫裡 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會說 , 生命是電擊器 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須要調節它 , 我在想我們要如何在二十一世紀創造安全 , 有時候我們會用真正的戰爭和危機來實現它 , 但會有很多例子 , 如同我們今天所說的 , 我們的軍隊可以成為創造二十一世紀安全的一部分 , 國際安全 , 跨部門 , 公共 , 和公共的 , 和密切的溝通 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後 , 我會說我們今天早先聽說過維基百科 。 我經常使用維基百科來查看事實 , 你們都很感激 , 維基百科不是被十二位傑出的人鎖在房間裡寫文章 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天有數萬人在輸入資訊 , 數百萬人在提取資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	這是我們所有人一起思考的完美圖像 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有我們所有人一起思考的那麼聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的宣言很簡單:在這個世界裡每個人都可以自由地分享所有知識 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 通過結合國際、跨部門、私人、戰略溝通 , 加在一起 , 在21世紀 , 我們就能創造出所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常謝謝 。 謝謝 。
